Source Code

These source-code files were derived from scans of the Colossus 237 (Apollo 8 Command Module) program listing from the private collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. Scanning was by Ron Burkey. Pre-existing Colossus 249 (Apollo 9 CM) source files were used as a template, and changes between Colossus 249 and Colossus 237 were manually transcribed by a team of volunteers. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 237 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS 
	BY NASA 2021111-031  1:17 AUG. 24, 1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

001439,000024: 
001440,000025:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001441,000026: 
001442,000027:                                                                                                  #           EQUALS IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001443,000028:                                                                                                  #                  OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001444,000029:                                                                                                  #                  CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001445,000030: 
001446,000031:                                                                                                  #                                          X        EQUALS START
001447,000032:                                                                                                  #                                          Y        EQUALS X        +SIZE.X
001448,000033:                                                                                                  #                                          Z        EQUALS Y        +SIZE.Y
001449,000034: 
001450,000035:                                                                                                  #                  (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001451,000036:                                                                                                  #                  (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001452,000037:                                                                                                  #                   USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001453,000038: 
001454,000039:                                                                                                  #           EQUALS OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001455,000040:                                                                                                  #                  AND DIFFERENT DATA). EXAMPLE.
001456,000041: 
001457,000042:                                                                                                  #                                          X        EQUALS Y
001458,000043: 
001459,000044:                                                                                                  #           = MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001460,000045:                                                                                                  #                  (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001461,000046: 
001462,000047:                                                                                                  #                                          X        =      Y
001463,000048: 
001464,000049:                                                                                                  #           THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001465,000050:                                                                                                  #           THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001466,000051: 
001467,000052:                                                                                                  #                  M REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001468,000053:                                                                                                  #                       B   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001469,000054:                                                                                                  #                           INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001470,000055:                                                                                                  #                       I   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001471,000056:                                                                                                  #                           INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001472,000057:                                                                                                  #                           INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001473,000058: 
001474,000059:                                                                                                  #                  SIZE IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001475,000060: 
001476,000061:                                                                                                  #                  N INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001477,000062:                                                                                                  #                       PL MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001478,000063:                                                                                                  #                       DSP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001479,000064:                                                                                                  #                       PRM MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001480,000065:                                                                                                  #                           IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001481,000066:                                                                                                  #                           PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001482,000067:                                                                                                  #                       TMP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001483,000068:                                                                                                  #                           IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001484,000069:                                                                                                  #                           IT IS ASSIGNED. THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001485,000070:                                                                                                  #                           PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001486,000071:                                                                                                  #                           CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 35 

001488,000073:                                                                                                  #                           IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001489,000074:                                                                                                  #                           IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001490,000075:                                                                                                  #                       IN  MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001491,000076:                                                                                                  #                           TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001492,000077:                                                                                                  #                       OUT MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001493,000078:                                                                                                  #                           TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001494,000079:

Page 36 

001496,000081: 
001497,000082:                                                                                                  #           SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001498,000083: 
001499,000084: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001500,000085: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001501,000086: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001502,000087: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001503,000088: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001504,000089: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001505,000090: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001506,000091:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001507,000092: 
001508,000093: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001509,000094: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001510,000095: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001511,000096: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001512,000097: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001513,000098: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001514,000099: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001515,000100: 
001516,000101: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20                                    
001517,000102: 37,2001                        SR                 EQUALS   21                                    
001518,000103: 37,2001                        CYL                EQUALS   22                                    
001519,000104: 37,2001                        EDOP               EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.
001520,000105: 
001521,000106: 37,2001                        TIME2              EQUALS   24                                    
001522,000107: 37,2001                        TIME1              EQUALS   25                                    
001523,000108: 37,2001                        TIME3              EQUALS   26                                    
001524,000109: 37,2001                        TIME4              EQUALS   27                                    
001525,000110: 37,2001                        TIME5              EQUALS   30                                    
001526,000111: 37,2001                        TIME6              EQUALS   31                                    
001527,000112: 37,2001                        CDUX               EQUALS   32                                    
001528,000113: 37,2001                        CDUY               EQUALS   33                                    
001529,000114: 37,2001                        CDUZ               EQUALS   34                                    
001530,000115: 37,2001                        CDUT               EQUALS   35                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION CDU (WAS OPTY).
001531,000116: 37,2001  0000035               OPTY               =        CDUT                                  
001532,000117: 37,2001                        CDUS               EQUALS   36                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT CDU (WAS OPTX).
001533,000118: 37,2001  0000036               OPTX               =        CDUS                                  
001534,000119: 37,2001                        PIPAX              EQUALS   37                                    
001535,000120: 37,2001                        PIPAY              EQUALS   40                                    
001536,000121: 37,2001                        PIPAZ              EQUALS   41                                    
001537,000122: 37,2001                        BMAGX              EQUALS   42                                    
001538,000123: 37,2001                        BMAGY              EQUALS   43                                    
001539,000124: 37,2001                        BMAGZ              EQUALS   44                                    
001540,000125: 37,2001                        INLINK             EQUALS   45                                    
001541,000126: 37,2001                        RNRAD              EQUALS   46                                    
001542,000127: 37,2001                        GYROCTR            EQUALS   47                                    
001543,000128: 37,2001                        GYROCMD            EQUALS   47                                    
001544,000129: 37,2001                        CDUXCMD            EQUALS   50                                    
001545,000130: 37,2001                        CDUYCMD            EQUALS   51

001547,000132: 37,2001                        CDUZCMD            EQUALS   52                                    
001548,000133: 37,2001                        CDUTCMD            EQUALS   53                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION COMMAND (WAS OPTYCMD).
001549,000134: 37,2001  0000053               OPTYCMD            =        CDUTCMD                               
001550,000135: 37,2001  0000053               TVCYAW             EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE.

002900,001485:                                                                                                  #           INTERRUPT TEMPORARY STORAGE POOL.  (11D)
002901,001486:                                                                                                  #             (ITEMP1 THROUGH RUPTREG4)          
002902,001487: 
002903,001488:                                                                                                  #           ANY OF THESE MAY BE USED AS TEMPORARIES DURING INTERRUPT OR WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED. THE ITEMP SERIES
002904,001489:                                                                                                  #  IS USED DURING CALLS TO THE EXECUTIVE AND WAITLIST - THE RUPTREGS ARE NOT.

002960,001545:

002972,001557:

002975,001560:    0130     0122               NOUNTEM            EQUALS   VBUF                                  #  COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH

002977,001562:    0130     0122               DECTEM             EQUALS   VBUF                                  #  COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
002978,001563:
